
---==============================
--L卡评分，获取信贷合同数据（过滤无效合同、只包含tnh和yfq产品）	  
--===================================
create table lkl_card_score_credit_type_user as 
select u.mobile,
t.loan_card_pan,
c.capital_limit, 
t.out_range,
case when substr(c.product_no,1,2) in ('PA','PJ') then 'tnh' 
     else 'yfq' end as product_type,
t.PAY_TIME,
c.start_date,
c.due_date,
c.contract_no 
 from creditloan.s_c_loan_apply  a 
inner join creditloan.s_c_apply_user u on u.id = a.id
inner join creditloan.s_c_loan_contract c on c.apply_id = a.id 
inner join creditloan.s_c_receipt t on t.contract_id = c.id 
where a.year='2017' and a.month='03' and a.day='06'
and u.year='2017' and u.month='03' and u.day='06'
and c.year='2017' and c.month='03' and c.day='06'
and t.year='2017' and t.month='03' and t.day='06'
and c.status <> 'F'
and substr(c.product_no,1,2) in ('PA','PJ','PC','PK')
and t.pay_time <> 'null';	


--L卡评分，获取phone最新合同数据 579437
--分产品：yfq、tnh
--======================================================
create table lkl_card_score_phone_user_yfq as
select 
	b.mobile,
	b.capital_limit, 
	b.out_range,
	b.product_type,
	b.PAY_TIME,
	b.start_date,
	b.due_date,
	b.contract_no
 from (
select 
    a.*
from
  (
	  select mobile ,PAY_TIME,row_number() over (partition by mobile order by PAY_TIME desc ) rank  
	   from lkl_card_score_credit_type_user
	   where PAY_TIME <> 'null'
	   group by mobile,PAY_TIME
  )a
where a.rank=1) tab,lkl_card_score_credit_type_user b
where tab.mobile = b.mobile
and tab.pay_time = b.pay_time
and b.product_type = 'yfq';

--产品 tnh
create table lkl_card_score_phone_user_tnh as
select 
	b.mobile,
	b.capital_limit, 
	b.out_range,
	b.product_type,
	b.PAY_TIME,
	b.start_date,
	b.due_date,
	b.contract_no
 from (
select 
    a.*
from
  (
	  select mobile ,PAY_TIME,row_number() over (partition by mobile order by PAY_TIME desc ) rank  
	   from lkl_card_score_credit_type_user
	   where PAY_TIME <> 'null'
	   group by mobile,PAY_TIME
  )a
where a.rank=1) tab,lkl_card_score_credit_type_user b
where tab.mobile = b.mobile
and tab.pay_time = b.pay_time
and b.product_type = 'tnh';

--=======================================================
--按时间分群
create table lkl_card_score_phone_variable_yfq_trainingdata_2016 as 
select b.gbie as label,t.PAY_TIME,
a.* from lkl_card_score_phone_user_yfq t 
join lkl_card_score_phone_variable_yfq a on t.mobile = a.phone
join lkl_card_score_credit_contract b on t.contract_no = b.contract_no
where b.gbie <> 0.5
and b.type ='yfq'
and substr(t.PAY_TIME,1,4) = '2016';

--========================================================
--训练数据 手机号

create table lkl_card_score_phone_variable_yfq_trainingdata as
select b.gbie as label,
a.* from lkl_card_score_phone_user_yfq t 
join lkl_card_score_phone_variable_yfq a on t.mobile = a.phone
join lkl_card_score_credit_contract b on t.contract_no = b.contract_no
where b.gbie <> 0.5
and b.type ='yfq';

create table lkl_card_score_phone_variable_tnh_trainingdata as
select b.gbie as label,
a.* from lkl_card_score_phone_user_tnh t 
join lkl_card_score_phone_variable_tnh a on t.mobile = a.phone
join lkl_card_score_credit_contract b on t.contract_no = b.contract_no
where b.gbie <> 0.5
and b.type ='tnh';

--训练数据 银行卡号 
create table lkl_card_score_acctno_variable_yfq_trainingdata as
select b.gbie as label,
a.* from lkl_card_score_acctno_user_yfq t 
join lkl_card_score_acctno_variable_yfq a on t.acctno = a.acctno
join lkl_card_score_credit_contract b on t.contract_no = b.contract_no
where b.gbie <> 0.5
and b.type ='yfq';

create table lkl_card_score_acctno_variable_tnh_trainingdata as
select b.gbie as label,
a.* from lkl_card_score_acctno_user_tnh t 
join lkl_card_score_acctno_variable_tnh a on t.acctno = a.acctno
join lkl_card_score_credit_contract b on t.contract_no = b.contract_no
where b.gbie <> 0.5
and b.type ='tnh';

--L卡评分，获取acctno最新合同数据  697508
--分产品：yfq、tnh
--=========================================================
create table lkl_card_score_acctno_user_yfq as
select 
	b.loan_card_pan as acctno,
	b.capital_limit, 
	b.out_range,
	b.product_type,
	b.PAY_TIME,
	b.start_date,
	b.due_date,
	b.contract_no
 from (
select 
    a.*
from
  (
	  select loan_card_pan ,PAY_TIME,row_number() over (partition by loan_card_pan order by PAY_TIME desc ) rank  
	   from lkl_card_score_credit_type_user
	   where PAY_TIME <> 'null'
	   group by loan_card_pan,PAY_TIME
  )a
where a.rank=1) tab,lkl_card_score_credit_type_user b
where tab.loan_card_pan = b.loan_card_pan
and tab.pay_time = b.pay_time
and b.product_type = 'yfq';

--分产品
create table lkl_card_score_acctno_user_tnh as
select 
	b.loan_card_pan as acctno,
	b.capital_limit, 
	b.out_range,
	b.product_type,
	b.PAY_TIME,
	b.start_date,
	b.due_date,
	b.contract_no
 from (
select 
    a.*
from
  (
	  select loan_card_pan ,PAY_TIME,row_number() over (partition by loan_card_pan order by PAY_TIME desc ) rank  
	   from lkl_card_score_credit_type_user
	   where PAY_TIME <> 'null'
	   group by loan_card_pan,PAY_TIME
  )a
where a.rank=1) tab,lkl_card_score_credit_type_user b
where tab.loan_card_pan = b.loan_card_pan
and tab.pay_time = b.pay_time
and b.product_type = 'tnh';

--替你还、易分期信贷数据分布
select product_type,substr(pay_time,1,7),count(*) from lkl_card_score_phone_user
group by product_type,substr(pay_time,1,7);

select product_type,substr(pay_time,1,7),count(*) from lkl_card_score_acctno_user
group by product_type,substr(pay_time,1,7);

--获取信贷合同所有交易流水数据
--银行卡号  8697507
select count(distinct acctno) from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_acctno ;  --695294
--====================================================================
set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create table lkl_card_score_trade_flow_acctno_yfq as
select 
 a.acctno,    --交易账号
 a.begintime, --开始时间
 a.endtime,   --结束时间
 a.amount,    --金额
 a.fee,       --交易服务费
 b.busid,     --交易小类 id
 b.busname,   --交易小类名称
 c.bustype,   --交易中类
 c.buscode,	  --交易中类code
 d.PAY_TIME  --信贷合同放款日期
 from lmps.s_tbl_tradelog a 
 join lmps.s_tbl_businfo b on a.busid = b.busid
 join lmps.customer_identifier_tradetype_base c on a.busid = c.busid 
 join lkl_card_score_acctno_user_yfq d on d.acctno = a.acctno
 where a.retcode = '00'
 and a.amount <> 'null'
 and a.acctno <> 'null'
 and a.endtime < d.pay_time
 and a.endtime >= date_sub(d.pay_time,730);
 
 
--产品
set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create table lkl_card_score_trade_flow_acctno_tnh as
select 
 a.acctno,    --交易账号
 a.begintime, --开始时间
 a.endtime,   --结束时间
 a.amount,    --金额
 a.fee,       --交易服务费
 b.busid,     --交易小类 id
 b.busname,   --交易小类名称
 c.bustype,   --交易中类
 c.buscode,	  --交易中类code
 d.PAY_TIME  --信贷合同放款日期
 from lmps.s_tbl_tradelog a 
 join lmps.s_tbl_businfo b on a.busid = b.busid
 join lmps.customer_identifier_tradetype_base c on a.busid = c.busid 
 join lkl_card_score_acctno_user_tnh d on d.acctno = a.acctno
 where a.retcode = '00'
 and a.amount <> 'null'
 and a.acctno <> 'null'
 and a.endtime < d.pay_time
 and a.endtime >= date_sub(d.pay_time,730);
 
--手机号 32866450
select count(distinct phone) from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_phone; --577369

set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create table lkl_card_score_trade_flow_phone_yfq as
select 
 a.contact as phone,    --手机号
 a.begintime, --开始时间
 a.endtime,   --结束时间
 a.amount,    --金额
 a.fee,       --交易服务费
 b.busid,     --交易小类 id
 b.busname,   --交易小类名称
 c.bustype,   --交易中类
 c.buscode,	  --交易中类code
 d.PAY_TIME  --信贷合同放款日期
 from lmps.s_tbl_tradelog a 
 join lmps.s_tbl_businfo b on a.busid = b.busid
 join lmps.customer_identifier_tradetype_base c on a.busid = c.busid 
 join lkl_card_score_phone_user_yfq d on d.mobile = a.contact
 where a.retcode = '00'
 and a.amount <> 'null'
 and a.contact <> 'null'
 and a.endtime < d.pay_time
 and a.endtime > date_sub(d.pay_time,730); 
 
 
 --分产品
 set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create table lkl_card_score_trade_flow_phone_tnh as
select 
 a.contact as phone,    --手机号
 a.begintime, --开始时间
 a.endtime,   --结束时间
 a.amount,    --金额
 a.fee,       --交易服务费
 b.busid,     --交易小类 id
 b.busname,   --交易小类名称
 c.bustype,   --交易中类
 c.buscode,	  --交易中类code
 d.PAY_TIME  --信贷合同放款日期
 from lmps.s_tbl_tradelog a 
 join lmps.s_tbl_businfo b on a.busid = b.busid
 join lmps.customer_identifier_tradetype_base c on a.busid = c.busid 
 join lkl_card_score_phone_user_tnh d on d.mobile = a.contact
 where a.retcode = '00'
 and a.amount <> 'null'
 and a.contact <> 'null'
 and a.endtime < d.pay_time
 and a.endtime > date_sub(d.pay_time,730); 
 

 --=========================
 --合同期 -- 替你还 1501-1701、易分期 为1506-1611
 --=========================
 --手机号
create table lkl_card_score_phone_peroid_yfq as
 select phone,amount/100 as amount,bustype,buscode,endtime,pay_time,
 (month(pay_time)-month(endtime) )+(year(pay_time)-year(endtime))*12 as peroid
 from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_phone_yfq a;
 
create table lkl_card_score_phone_peroid_tnh as
 select phone,amount/100 as amount,bustype,buscode,endtime,pay_time,
 (month(pay_time)-month(endtime) )+(year(pay_time)-year(endtime))*12 as peroid
 from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_phone_tnh a;
 
 
--银行卡号 
 create table lkl_card_score_acctno_peroid_yfq as
 select acctno,amount/100 as amount,bustype,buscode,endtime,pay_time,
 (month(pay_time)-month(endtime) )+(year(pay_time)-year(endtime))*12 as peroid
 from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_acctno_yfq a;
 
 create table lkl_card_score_acctno_peroid_tnh as
 select acctno,amount/100 as amount,bustype,buscode,endtime,pay_time,
 (month(pay_time)-month(endtime) )+(year(pay_time)-year(endtime))*12 as peroid
 from lkl_card_score_trade_flow_acctno_tnh a; 
 
--分组统计 手机号  33313067

set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create table lkl_card_score_phone_peroid_statistic_yfq as
select phone,buscode,sum(amount) as sum_amount,avg(amount) as avg_amount,max(amount) as max_amount,min(amount) as min_amount,count(1) as sum_cnt, 1 as peroid 
from lkl_card_score_phone_peroid_yfq
where peroid = 1
group by phone,buscode
union all  
select phone,buscode,sum(amount) as sum_amount,avg(amount) as avg_amount,max(amount) as max_amount,min(amount) as min_amount,count(1) as sum_cnt, 2 as peroid 
from lkl_card_score_phone_peroid_yfq

--行转列 手机号码
set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

insert overwrite  table lkl_card_score_query_phone_tag_yfq
select 
    phone,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 1 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount1_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 1 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount1_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 1 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount1_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 1 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount1_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 1 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt1_enquiryBalance,
    sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 2 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount2_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 2 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount2_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 2 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount2_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 2 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount2_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 2 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt2_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 3 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount3_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 3 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount3_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 3 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount3_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 3 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount3_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 3 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt3_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 4 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount4_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 4 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount4_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 4 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount4_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 4 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount4_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 4 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt4_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 5 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount5_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 5 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount5_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 5 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount5_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 5 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount5_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 5 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt5_enquiryBalance,
    sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 6 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount6_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 6 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount6_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 6 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount6_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 6 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount6_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 6 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt6_enquiryBalance,
	sum(case when buscode = 'enquiryBalance' and peroid = 7 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount7_enquiryBalance,

set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create  table lkl_card_score_publicPay_phone_tag_yfq as
select 
    phone,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 1 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount1_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 1 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount1_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 1 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount1_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 1 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount1_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 1 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt1_electricityFee,
    sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 2 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount2_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 2 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount2_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 2 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount2_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 2 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount2_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 2 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt2_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 3 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount3_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 3 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount3_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 3 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount3_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 3 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount3_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 3 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt3_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 4 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount4_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 4 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount4_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 4 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount4_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 4 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount4_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 4 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt4_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 5 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount5_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 5 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount5_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 5 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount5_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 5 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount5_electricityFee,
	sum(case when buscode = 'electricityFee' and peroid = 5 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt5_electricityFee,

set hive.exec.parallel=8;
set hive.exec.reducers.max=200;
set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

create  table lkl_card_score_auth_acctno_tag_yfq as
select 
    acctno,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 1 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount1_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 1 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount1_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 1 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount1_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 1 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount1_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 1 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt1_authentication,
    sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 2 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount2_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 2 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount2_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 2 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount2_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 2 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount2_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 2 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt2_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 3 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount3_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 3 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount3_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 3 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount3_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 3 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount3_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 3 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt3_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 4 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount4_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 4 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount4_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 4 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount4_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 4 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount4_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 4 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt4_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 5 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount5_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 5 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount5_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 5 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount5_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 5 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount5_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 5 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt5_authentication,
    sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 6 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount6_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 6 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount6_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 6 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount6_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 6 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount6_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 6 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt6_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 7 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount7_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 7 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount7_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 7 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount7_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 7 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount7_authentication,
	sum(case when buscode = 'authentication' and peroid = 7 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt7_authentication,

	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 23 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount23_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 23 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount23_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 23 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount23_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 23 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt23_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 24 then sum_amount else 0 end) as sum_amount24_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 24 then avg_amount else 0 end) as avg_amount24_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 24 then max_amount else 0 end) as max_amount24_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 24 then min_amount else 0 end) as min_amount24_lottery,
	sum(case when buscode = 'lottery' and peroid = 24 then sum_cnt    else 0 end) as    sum_cnt24_lottery
from lkl_card_score_acctno_peroid_statistic_yfq
where buscode in ('authentication','acquiring','confirmation','lottery')
group by acctno;

set mapred.reduce.tasks= 200;

left join lkl_card_score_publicPay_phone_tag_yfq d on a.phone = d.phone

left join lkl_card_score_auth_phone_tag_yfq f on a.phone = f.phone
left join lkl_card_score_credit_phone_tag_yfq g on a.phone = g.phone
left join lkl_card_score_recharge_phone_tag_yfq h on a.phone = h.phone;

(avg_amount1_creditCardRepayments  +
